\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00073}00073 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00074}00074 \textcolor{comment}{// (Read carefully because this is subtle but it does make sense!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00075}00075 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00076}00076 \textcolor{comment}{// About 'outer\_size':}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{// Its meaning needs to differ slightly depending on if we are using ScrollX/ScrollY flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{// Default value is ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{//   X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00080}00080 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.x <= 0.0f  -\/>  Right-\/align from window/work-\/rect right-\/most edge. With -\/FLT\_MIN or 0.0f will align exactly on right-\/most edge.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00081}00081 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.x  > 0.0f  -\/>  Set Fixed width.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00082}00082 \textcolor{comment}{//   Y with ScrollX/ScrollY disabled: we output table directly in current window}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.y  < 0.0f  -\/>  Bottom-\/align (but will auto extend, unless \_NoHostExtendY is set). Not meaningful is parent window can vertically scroll.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00084}00084 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.y  = 0.0f  -\/>  No minimum height (but will auto extend, unless \_NoHostExtendY is set)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.y  > 0.0f  -\/>  Set Minimum height (but will auto extend, unless \_NoHostExtenY is set)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{//   Y with ScrollX/ScrollY enabled: using a child window for scrolling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00087}00087 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.y  < 0.0f  -\/>  Bottom-\/align. Not meaningful is parent window can vertically scroll.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.y  = 0.0f  -\/>  Bottom-\/align, consistent with BeginChild(). Not recommended unless table is last item in parent window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ outer\_size.y  > 0.0f  -\/>  Set Exact height. Recommended when using Scrolling on any axis.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00091}00091 \textcolor{comment}{// Outer size is also affected by the NoHostExtendX/NoHostExtendY flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{// Important to that note how the two flags have slightly different behaviors!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendX -\/> Make outer width auto-\/fit to columns (overriding outer\_size.x value). Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY are disabled and Stretch columns are not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00094}00094 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendY -\/> Make outer height stop exactly at outer\_size.y (prevent auto-\/extending table past the limit). Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY is disabled. Data below the limit will be clipped and not visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{// In theory ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendY could be the default and any non-\/scrolling tables with outer\_size.y != 0.0f would use exact height.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{// This would be consistent but perhaps less useful and more confusing (as vertically clipped items are not easily noticeable)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{// About 'inner\_width':}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{//   With ScrollX disabled:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ inner\_width          -\/>  *ignored*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{//   With ScrollX enabled:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ inner\_width  < 0.0f  -\/>  *illegal* fit in known width (right align from outer\_size.x) <-\/-\/ weird}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ inner\_width  = 0.0f  -\/>  fit in outer\_width: Fixed size columns will take space they need (if avail, otherwise shrink down), Stretch columns becomes Fixed columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ inner\_width  > 0.0f  -\/>  override scrolling width, generally to be larger than outer\_size.x. Fixed column take space they need (if avail, otherwise shrink down), Stretch columns share remaining space!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{// Details:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you want to use Stretch columns with ScrollX, you generally need to specify 'inner\_width' otherwise the concept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{//   of "{}available space"{} doesn't make sense.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Even if not really useful, we allow 'inner\_width < outer\_size.x' for consistency and to facilitate understanding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{//   of what the value does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00112}00112 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{// COLUMNS SIZING POLICIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{// About overriding column sizing policy and width/weight with TableSetupColumn():}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{// We use a default parameter of 'init\_width\_or\_weight == -\/1'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed,    init\_width  <= 0 (default)  -\/-\/> width is automatic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed,    init\_width  >  0 (explicit) -\/-\/> width is custom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch,  init\_weight <= 0 (default)  -\/-\/> weight is 1.0f}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch,  init\_weight >  0 (explicit) -\/-\/> weight is custom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{// Widths are specified \_without\_ CellPadding. If you specify a width of 100.0f, the column will be cover (100.0f + Padding * 2.0f)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{// and you can fit a 100.0f wide item in it without clipping and with full padding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{// About default sizing policy (if you don't specify a ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthXXXX flag)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with Table policy ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit      -\/-\/> default Column policy is ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed, default Width is equal to contents width}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with Table policy ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame     -\/-\/> default Column policy is ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed, default Width is max of all contents width}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with Table policy ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame   -\/-\/> default Column policy is ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch, default Weight is 1.0f}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ with Table policy ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchWeight -\/-\/> default Column policy is ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch, default Weight is proportional to contents}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{// Default Width and default Weight can be overridden when calling TableSetupColumn().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{// About mixing Fixed/Auto and Stretch columns together:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ the typical use of mixing sizing policies is: any number of LEADING Fixed columns, followed by one or two TRAILING Stretch columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ using mixed policies with ScrollX does not make much sense, as using Stretch columns with ScrollX does not make much sense in the first place!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{//     that is, unless 'inner\_width' is passed to BeginTable() to explicitly provide a total width to layout columns in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ when using ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame with mixed columns, only the Fixed/Auto columns will match their widths to the width of the maximum contents.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ when using ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame with mixed columns, only the Stretch columns will match their weight/widths.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{// About using column width:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{// If a column is manual resizable or has a width specified with TableSetupColumn():}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ you may use GetContentRegionAvail().x to query the width available in a given column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00142}00142 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ right-\/side alignment features such as SetNextItemWidth(-\/x) or PushItemWidth(-\/x) will rely on this width.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{// If the column is not resizable and has no width specified with TableSetupColumn():}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ its width will be automatic and be set to the max of items submitted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00145}00145 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ therefore you generally cannot have ALL items of the columns use e.g. SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ but if the column has one or more items of known/fixed size, this will become the reference width used by SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00148}00148 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00149}00149 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00150}00150 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00151}00151 \textcolor{comment}{// TABLES CLIPPING/CULLING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00152}00152 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00153}00153 \textcolor{comment}{// About clipping/culling of Rows in Tables:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For large numbers of rows, it is recommended you use ImGuiListClipper to only submit visible rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00155}00155 \textcolor{comment}{//   ImGuiListClipper is reliant on the fact that rows are of equal height.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{//   See 'Demo-\/>Tables-\/>Vertical Scrolling' or 'Demo-\/>Tables-\/>Advanced' for a demo of using the clipper.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Note that auto-\/resizing columns don't play well with using the clipper.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{//   By default a table with \_ScrollX but without \_Resizable will have column auto-\/resize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{//   So, if you want to use the clipper, make sure to either enable \_Resizable, either setup columns width explicitly with \_WidthFixed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{// About clipping/culling of Columns in Tables:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00162}00162 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Both TableSetColumnIndex() and TableNextColumn() return true when the column is visible or performing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00163}00163 \textcolor{comment}{//   width measurements. Otherwise, you may skip submitting the contents of a cell/column, BUT ONLY if you know}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00164}00164 \textcolor{comment}{//   it is not going to contribute to row height.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00165}00165 \textcolor{comment}{//   In many situations, you may skip submitting contents for every column but one (e.g. the first one).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00166}00166 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Case A: column is not hidden by user, and at least partially in sight (most common case).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00167}00167 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Case B: column is clipped / out of sight (because of scrolling or parent ClipRect): TableNextColumn() return false as a hint but we still allow layout output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Case C: column is hidden explicitly by the user (e.g. via the context menu, or \_DefaultHide column flag, etc.).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00169}00169 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00170}00170 \textcolor{comment}{//                        [A]         [B]          [C]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00171}00171 \textcolor{comment}{//  TableNextColumn():    true        false        false       -\/> [userland] when TableNextColumn() / TableSetColumnIndex() return false, user can skip submitting items but only if the column doesn't contribute to row height.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00172}00172 \textcolor{comment}{//          SkipItems:    false       false        true        -\/> [internal] when SkipItems is true, most widgets will early out if submitted, resulting is no layout output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00173}00173 \textcolor{comment}{//           ClipRect:    normal      zero-\/width   zero-\/width  -\/> [internal] when ClipRect is zero, ItemAdd() will return false and most widgets will early out mid-\/way.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00174}00174 \textcolor{comment}{//  ImDrawList output:    normal      dummy        dummy       -\/> [internal] when using the dummy channel, ImDrawList submissions (if any) will be wasted (because cliprect is zero-\/width anyway).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00175}00175 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00176}00176 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We need to distinguish those cases because non-\/hidden columns that are clipped outside of scrolling bounds should still contribute their height to the row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00177}00177 \textcolor{comment}{//   However, in the majority of cases, the contribution to row height is the same for all columns, or the tallest cells are known by the programmer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00178}00178 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00179}00179 \textcolor{comment}{// About clipping/culling of whole Tables:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00180}00180 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Scrolling tables with a known outer size can be clipped earlier as BeginTable() will return false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00181}00181 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00182}00182 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00183}00183 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l00184}00184 \textcolor{comment}{// [SECTION] Header mess}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02238}02238 \textcolor{comment}{// Allocate draw channels. Called by TableUpdateLayout()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02239}02239 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We allocate them following storage order instead of display order so reordering columns won't needlessly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02240}02240 \textcolor{comment}{//   increase overall dormant memory cost.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02241}02241 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We isolate headers draw commands in their own channels instead of just altering clip rects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02242}02242 \textcolor{comment}{//   This is in order to facilitate merging of draw commands.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02243}02243 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ After crossing FreezeRowsCount, all columns see their current draw channel changed to a second set of channels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02244}02244 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We only use the dummy draw channel so we can push a null clipping rectangle into it without affecting other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02245}02245 \textcolor{comment}{//   channels, while simplifying per-\/row/per-\/cell overhead. It will be empty and discarded when merged.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02246}02246 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We allocate 1 or 2 background draw channels. This is because we know TablePushBackgroundChannel() is only used for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02247}02247 \textcolor{comment}{//   horizontal spanning. If we allowed vertical spanning we'd need one background draw channel per merge group (1-\/4).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02248}02248 \textcolor{comment}{// Draw channel allocation (before merging):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02249}02249 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ NoClip                       -\/-\/> 2+D+1 channels: bg0/1 + bg2 + foreground (same clip rect == always 1 draw call)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02250}02250 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clip                         -\/-\/> 2+D+N channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02251}02251 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ FreezeRows                   -\/-\/> 2+D+N*2 (unless scrolling value is zero)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02252}02252 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ FreezeRows || FreezeColunns  -\/-\/> 3+D+N*2 (unless scrolling value is zero)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02253}02253 \textcolor{comment}{// Where D is 1 if any column is clipped or hidden (dummy channel) otherwise 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02254}02254 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} ImGui::TableSetupDrawChannels(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_table}{ImGuiTable}}* \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02255}02255 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02256}02256     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} freeze\_row\_multiplier = (\mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>FreezeRowsCount > 0) ? 2 : 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02257}02257     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channels\_for\_row = (\mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>Flags \& ImGuiTableFlags\_NoClip) ? 1 : \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>ColumnsEnabledCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02258}02258     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channels\_for\_bg = 1 + 1 * freeze\_row\_multiplier;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02259}02259     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channels\_for\_dummy = (\mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>ColumnsEnabledCount < \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>ColumnsCount || \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>VisibleMaskByIndex != \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>EnabledMaskByIndex) ? +1 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02260}02260     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channels\_total = channels\_for\_bg + (channels\_for\_row * freeze\_row\_multiplier) + channels\_for\_dummy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02261}02261     \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>DrawSplitter-\/>Split(\mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>InnerWindow-\/>DrawList, channels\_total);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02262}02262     \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>DummyDrawChannel = (ImGuiTableDrawChannelIdx)((channels\_for\_dummy > 0) ? channels\_total -\/ 1 : -\/1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02263}02263     \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>Bg2DrawChannelCurrent = TABLE\_DRAW\_CHANNEL\_BG2\_FROZEN;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02264}02264     \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>Bg2DrawChannelUnfrozen = (ImGuiTableDrawChannelIdx)((\mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>FreezeRowsCount > 0) ? 2 + channels\_for\_row : TABLE\_DRAW\_CHANNEL\_BG2\_FROZEN);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02265}02265 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02266}02266     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} draw\_channel\_current = 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02267}02267     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = 0; column\_n < \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}}-\/>ColumnsCount; column\_n++)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02283}02283 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02284}02284     \textcolor{comment}{// Initial draw cmd starts with a BgClipRect that matches the one of its host, to facilitate merge draw commands by default.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02285}02285     \textcolor{comment}{// All our cell highlight are manually clipped with BgClipRect. When unfreezing it will be made smaller to fit scrolling rect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02286}02286     \textcolor{comment}{// (This technically isn't part of setting up draw channels, but is reasonably related to be done here)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02291}02291 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02292}02292 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02293}02293 \textcolor{comment}{// This function reorder draw channels based on matching clip rectangle, to facilitate merging them. Called by EndTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02294}02294 \textcolor{comment}{// For simplicity we call it TableMergeDrawChannels() but in fact it only reorder channels + overwrite ClipRect,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02295}02295 \textcolor{comment}{// actual merging is done by table-\/>DrawSplitter.Merge() which is called right after TableMergeDrawChannels().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02296}02296 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02297}02297 \textcolor{comment}{// Columns where the contents didn't stray off their local clip rectangle can be merged. To achieve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02298}02298 \textcolor{comment}{// this we merge their clip rect and make them contiguous in the channel list, so they can be merged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02299}02299 \textcolor{comment}{// by the call to DrawSplitter.Merge() following to the call to this function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02300}02300 \textcolor{comment}{// We reorder draw commands by arranging them into a maximum of 4 distinct groups:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02301}02301 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02302}02302 \textcolor{comment}{//   1 group:               2 groups:              2 groups:              4 groups:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02303}02303 \textcolor{comment}{//   [ 0. ] no freeze       [ 0. ] row freeze      [ 01 ] col freeze      [ 01 ] row+col freeze}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02304}02304 \textcolor{comment}{//   [ .. ]  or no scroll   [ 2. ]  and v-\/scroll   [ .. ]  and h-\/scroll   [ 23 ]  and v+h-\/scroll}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02305}02305 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02306}02306 \textcolor{comment}{// Each column itself can use 1 channel (row freeze disabled) or 2 channels (row freeze enabled).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02307}02307 \textcolor{comment}{// When the contents of a column didn't stray off its limit, we move its channels into the corresponding group}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02308}02308 \textcolor{comment}{// based on its position (within frozen rows/columns groups or not).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02309}02309 \textcolor{comment}{// At the end of the operation our 1-\/4 groups will each have a ImDrawCmd using the same ClipRect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02310}02310 \textcolor{comment}{// This function assume that each column are pointing to a distinct draw channel,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02311}02311 \textcolor{comment}{// otherwise merge\_group-\/>ChannelsCount will not match set bit count of merge\_group-\/>ChannelsMask.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02312}02312 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02313}02313 \textcolor{comment}{// Column channels will not be merged into one of the 1-\/4 groups in the following cases:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02314}02314 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The contents stray off its clipping rectangle (we only compare the MaxX value, not the MinX value).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02315}02315 \textcolor{comment}{//   Direct ImDrawList calls won't be taken into account by default, if you use them make sure the ImGui:: bounds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02316}02316 \textcolor{comment}{//   matches, by e.g. calling SetCursorScreenPos().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02317}02317 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The channel uses more than one draw command itself. We drop all our attempt at merging stuff here..}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02318}02318 \textcolor{comment}{//   we could do better but it's going to be rare and probably not worth the hassle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02319}02319 \textcolor{comment}{// Columns for which the draw channel(s) haven't been merged with other will use their own ImDrawCmd.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02320}02320 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02321}02321 \textcolor{comment}{// This function is particularly tricky to understand.. take a breath.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02322}02322 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} ImGui::TableMergeDrawChannels(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_table}{ImGuiTable}}* \mbox{\hyperlink{structtable}{table}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02323}02323 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02790}02790     \textcolor{comment}{// Caring for a minor edge case:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02791}02791     \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate row height, for the unlikely case that some labels may be taller than others.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02792}02792     \textcolor{comment}{// If we didn't do that, uneven header height would highlight but smaller one before the tallest wouldn't catch input for all height.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02793}02793     \textcolor{comment}{// In your custom header row you may omit this all together and just call TableNextRow() without a height...}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02796}02796     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = 0; column\_n < columns\_count; column\_n++)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02800}02800             row\_height = ImMax(row\_height, CalcTextSize(TableGetColumnName(column\_n)).y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02801}02801     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02802}02802     row\_height += GetStyle().CellPadding.y * 2.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__tables_8cpp_source_l02803}02803     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} row\_height;}
